this output is for the doc : corr17.txt here is his output 
  
import json

resume = """
...paste the resume here...
"""

tables = [line.strip() for line in resume.split("\n") if "Tableau" in line]

table_8 = [line for line in tables if "Tableau 8:" in line][0]
table_9 = [line for line in tables if "Tableau 9:" in line][0]

location_table = table_8.split(":")[1].strip().split(",")
location = {"wilaya": "Tipaza", "latitude": location_table[0].strip(), "longitude": location_table[1].strip()}

parameters_table = table_9.split(":")[1].strip().split(",")
parameters = {
    "pH": float(parameters_table[0].strip()),
    "Calcaire Total": float(parameters_table[1].strip()),
    "Mati�re Organique (MO)": float(parameters_table[2].strip()),
    "Capacit� d'�change Cationique (CEC)": float(parameters_table[3].strip()),
    "Conductivit� �lectrique (CE)": float(parameters_table[4].strip()),
    "Densit� Apparente (Da)": float(parameters_table[5].strip())
}

depth_table = [line for line in tables if "Photo" in line and "Pr�l�vement de poids des �chantillons avant le s�chage" in line][0]
depth = depth_table.split(";")[1].strip().split("=")[1].strip()

result = {
    "location": location,
    "parameters": parameters,
    "depth": depth
}

print(json.dumps(result, indent=4))

    "Conductivit� �lectrique (CE)": "unknown", // Conductivit� �lectrique (CE) not found in the text

this output is for the doc : corr102.txt here is his output 
  Python
import json
import re

def extract_info(text):
    # Extract location information (wilaya, latitude, longitude, depth)
    location_pattern = r"(\d{2}\.\d{4})[�N, ]+(\d{3}\.\d{4})[�E, ]+(\d+) cm"
    match = re.search(location_pattern, text)
    if match:
        latitude, longitude, depth = match.groups()
        wilaya = "Wilaya of Mascara"  # Assuming the wilaya is not provided in the text
    else:
        latitude, longitude, wilaya, depth = "", "", "", ""

    # Extract soil parameters
    parameters_pattern = r"pH (\d+\.\d+),Calcaire Total (\d+\.\d+),Mati�re Organique \(MO\) (\d+\.\d+),Capacit� d'�change Cationique \(CEC\) (\d+\.\d+),Conductivit� �lectrique \(CE\) (\d+\.\d+),Densit� Apparente \(Da\) (\d+\.\d+)"
    match = re.search(parameters_pattern, text)
    if match:
        pH, calcaire_total, MO, CEC, CE, Da = match.groups()
    else:
        pH, calcaire_total, MO, CEC, CE, Da = "", "", "", "", "", ""

    # Create the JSON response
    response = {
        "location": {
            "wilaya": wilaya,
            "latitude": latitude,
            "longitude": longitude
        },
        "parameters": {
            "pH": pH,
            "Calcaire Total": calcaire_total,
            "Mati�re Organique (MO)": MO,
            "Capacit� d'�change Cationique (CEC)": CEC,
            "Conductivit� �lectrique (CE)": CE,
            "Densit� Apparente (Da)": Da
        },
        "depth": depth
    }

    return json.dumps(response)

text = """
... your text here ...
"""

print(extract_info(text))
